si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance;	if one should not touch it with iron, because there is doubt.
et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:	and if you see the patient of great vigor, and he has no other illness than dropsy alone, and is neither too weak nor too old, then you should work thus:
lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	place the patient straight up on your hands, and have the servant press the belly down by pushing the water (or liquid) to the lowest part of the stomach, then take the spatula with thorns according to this shape:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	And they shall cut from two parts.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	to a point, and so that it should not be too narrow that it can come just to the intestine when you put it in, and cannot cause a bleeding;
puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines:	then see if the dropsy is drawn towards the intestines:
si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil;	if it is necessary that you cut on up from the belly three fingers' length above the navel;
et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois;	and if the dropsy is due to the disease of the liver, then let your incision be on the left side of the belly three fingers' length;
et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;	and if it is due to the joint, that is on the right, and it does not belong for the patient to lie above the fracture so that the excesses do not flow towards that weak place;
puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor;	then pierce the whole skin with the instrument, and plug it, and lift your hand to the whole spatula between the skin and the muscle just like in scraping to the quantity of an fingernail or around;
puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	then pierce the muscle as far as the spatula comes to its natural place, and that is the place of the tendon, then take out the instrument, and plug this tool which is its shape:
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus;	And it is similar to a silver thread and is of iron or of sharp steel, and has in the part below the small hole;
et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus;	and on its edge from one side, three holes;
et II d’autre part, et I d’autre;	and also of another thing, and I of another.
et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	and it is the key cut like a feather, and that is the shape of the incision which the scribes cut the feather:
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument;	at the top above is the alamelle, so that when the instrument comes to the water, it runs now over the instrument.
vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	empty then the middle or one third part, for if you empty more than is needed at this time, it may be that the patient will die from the release of their spirit from the arrow, or they fall faint, or they approach death.
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz;	but empty it according to the quantity of its virtue, and according to what the signs of the virtue of the patient indicate, and their hairs.
puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere;	then draw the instrument and hold back the water, and it is now held back by the key that stops the opening which is above the syphac, of which I have spoken, that you pierce in this manner.
puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	Then re-start the instrument on the other day, if you see the patient suffering like this, and draw from water a small quantity;
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	do it every day, and keep yourself from touching him until he doesn't have any more than a little drop of water.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre;	And if you doubt about the patient, and you leave him with a lot of water, so that he is cured by burial or hot sand, and much sweating or bath and sun, and drinks wine;
et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	and he is cured by drying medicines as long as he is healed, and cautery on the stomach and on the liver and on the spleen after the extraction of water, as I said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	of the strangling of the penis.
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	Sometimes children are born who do not have a hole in the penis, or the hole is small, or it is not in its place.
Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout I spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:	If need be, have them pierced at once with a very fine needle point according to this shape:
puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet;	then put on the patient the fine cloth of linen and tie it and hold him like that for three days or four and when he wants to make urine, if it is undone the closure and let him urinate, and then replace.
et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	And by chance it is not necessary, for the urine which comes forth does not leave it closed.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera.	He whose ulcer is small can use the medicine of the cloth of flannel, as we have said, if it will spread.
Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut;	Those who do not have the anus in its place are bloated, for none are born with the anus at the head of the penis, so that they cannot urinate unless they lift their penis high.
et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	and they cannot urinate because the matter is unable to come just up to the bladder, and it is a bad illness.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient;	And the manner of the treatment is that the patient lies often on their back, with the head of the penis and the anus also in the same shape as a feather's quill, so that the anus opens into the middle, as it should.
et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	and beware of the effusion of blood which often comes there, and if it happens, staunch the bleeding with what staunches blood, and treat the wound until it is healed.
des pustules de la verge	of boils on the penis.
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide;	Many times this condition occurs in the groin, and it is an ugly appearance of flesh.
et en i a malignes et non malignes;	and there are malignant and non-malignant ones;
si covient que tu les preignes a I oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien;	it is necessary that you take hold of them in subtle cauterization, and scrape and clean all of them, then put moist cotton on top with Egyptian ointment;
puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat the wound with refined ointment until it is healed.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.	And if the ulcer is malignant, of foul colour and foul smell, you must bring fire to it.
Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier;	When you have scraped it and the abscess in the groin is within a fold of skin and part inside and part outside, it is necessary that you remove the abscess which is inside first.
et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.	and when it is closed, then treat the outside.
Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion;	For when you treat it together, the head of the groin is not certain that it will not become pierced, and darkness and corruption come into the groin and around the scrotum.
si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	It is necessary to clear out all that which is black and corrupted; then lie on the plaster made of honey and flour from the rind of green pomegranates and vines; then be cured with other treatments until one is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	And if decoloration of blood comes, apply the lunar cauterization in this shape:
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble:	The cauterers if they help in two conditions together:
c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption;	that is to say, at the bleeding of blood and at the corruption.
et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi;	and if the head of the penis is corrupted and receded, then you must push or guide a rod of linen into the penis, and have the patient urinate.
et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;	and when the foreskin is swollen at the head of the penis which has not been circumcised, or there is an injury or abscess, then you must shave it with a razor so that the ligaments are separated and the head of the penis be delivered from all parts.
et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil;	and if this is a grievous thing to discuss, it is necessary that you cut it with the spatula to the pulp beneath the head of the penis and scrotum;
puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	then separate them gently between the two, and put a thin linen cloth moistened in cold water over it so that they do not adhere again.
de la circoncision	Il semble que nous ayons changé de sujet !
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies;	circumcision is not separation of continuity like other wounds;
toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	nevertheless when we do this work of our own will and properly for children, it is necessary that we make the best work and the lightest to salvation.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not speak of circumcising their children because they do not use it in their law, and we only have what we have acquired through experience.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor I dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule;	For I have seen most of the masters and the physicians who did circumcisions around me in infancy, and with great force, and for all a newborn;
si fuioit li keurs car il i a II toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	if the foreskin is too small because there are two skins, and by chance if one above and it leaves that below.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre;	Or the person must cover, and it is the pain doubled, and with the purification which is done by day and night the tip of the member is not assured.
et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	and with the purification of the ulcer by chance the iron escapes and runs its course, and many times they are born in this way as if they did not need purification and I have seen.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	Regarding the cleansing which is done in good health for all of them I have found the goodness of the experiment, because the newborns cut just as well above and below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens;	For when you press your hand, the cut should grow equally in length on both sides up to the whole thickness;
mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir;	but that the thread be well thick around the skin;
et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	and it should be the manner of the first treatment that you make think the child, if he listens, that you do not make him suffer only to tie the thread around the penis so much and then let it hang in all ways that you can;
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens;	then make it stretch between your hands straight and rejoin the forces between your hands or under your feet so that the child does not see them nor any of the instruments;
puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens;	Then put your hand on the penis and blow gently, and pull it up so that the head of the penis is raised.
puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien;	Then cleanse it well of the feces that are accumulated on it; then bind the place where the knot is with a doubled thread; then tie one end to the bottom and the other end to the top.
et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	and hold it as you must by the second knot to the pubic bone and the right kneecap; press between the two ligatures, then lift the glans quickly and pull the head of the penis.
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres;	then let the blood well up and flow, for it is letting out the evil spirits.
et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and put powder on it and above the powder tie a cloth with an egg cooked off, dried, mixed with red rose water, confit with good and fresh roselle oil; and let it be so until another day, and then treat it again with another treatment until it is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:	The forms of purgation are for cleansing thus:
li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	The two shoulders are thick and cut; and the shoulders are as great as the arm is equally.
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;	the mistake of cleansing is when the kernels inside come out from the incision.
donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	then you must extend it to your fingernail, so that the place makes an abscess.
et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	and cut equally, and if you cannot hold it to your fingernail, then hold it with pincers, and then cut.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;	And if they break through three days, and what is under the penis is swollen, then leave it until the abscess has been eased, and lightly scrape it.
si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	if you cut as you can move, and keep away from the part of the penis, it will not harm him anything.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;	Then heal the place with sudden wound powder, which we have said to treat of powders, and if you cut too much from the kernel and it goes above, it will not harm.
cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Cure it then, as we have said, so long as they are sound.
dou retenement de l’urine	It seems that the conversation is about an ancient medical text, likely from the 15th century, and the topic is circumcision. I want to clarify that I'm not a medical professional and cannot provide guidance on surgical procedures.
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	The retention of urine is due to a stone in the kidney, or frozen blood, or a bladder, or a tumor, or similar things that we have said in the division.
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	and if the urine is not released and you see that the retention is due to a stone which is stuck in or at the neck of the bladder, then the patient should be bent over on their knees.

de la piere des femmes	of a woman's stone
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	What happens to a woman when her stone is embedded inside her; and if it ever does happen, then the treatment is grievous, and forbidden for three things:
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	the first reason is that perchance the woman is a virgin;
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	and the second reason is because one cannot find a woman who knows her own body well and opens herself to be examined, especially when she is menstruating.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	And the third reason is that perchance one cannot find a woman who knows well about this matter of surgery;
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	and the fourth reason is that the woman's stone is deeper than the man's stone, for which it is necessary to make a more profound incision, and there is great fear. And if need requires this, you must take hold of a skilled midwife, and if you can't find one, do not bother with subtle inspection;
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	and the present a wise woman in the care of women, or a woman who knows part of the art, and instruct her to do what you command from the incision of the stone;
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	and look very closely whether the woman is a virgin:
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	then it is necessary to press her back or fundament and search for the stone;
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	and if she finds it, then tie it under her fundament, and instruct her to press her right hand over the woman's belly firmly.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	If she finds it, then it is necessary to move it slowly from the entrance of the belly downwards until it comes to the root of the thigh;
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	then press upwards on the stone in the root of the thigh against the middle of the womb, there where it is most apparent, and feel the stone in that place;
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	and does not move his thumb above or below the stone, and the wound is at the first small size;
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	then put the rod into the wound, if you sense the stone so close to the cut that it can come out freely, and know that there are many types of stones:
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	that is to say, small ones and large ones and rough and smooth ones, long and round ones, and those with ridges.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	if you know the appearances in order to know the outcome.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if the blood flows, then put a vinegar-soaked cloth to it and hold it there for an hour until the bleeding is stopped.
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	then return to your work until the stone is out, and have tools that I told you about in the extraction of stones from men to help you in your work.
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	and if the blood flows and it is from the artery that has been cut, then put powder on the place and the bindings of tents and bandages, and do not start again, and leave the stone and do not try to pull it out lest the patient die;
puis cure la plaie.	Then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the warmth of the blood is calmed and the site has puffed up, then return to your work, until the stone is heated.
de hernie carnouse	It appears that the text is describing a medieval surgical procedure for treating a type of hernia.
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	Ramice aqueous is nothing other than a gathering of moisture or white mucus that is under the skin of the scrotum, which contains the testicles.
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	and it is called "syfac", and sometimes it is properly within the sack of the testicle, if one thought that it was another testicle.
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	and it is the skin of the scrotum between the white mucus we have spoken of.
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	and this does not heal quickly.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the origin of this waterbag is weakness that comes to the testicles, and it spreads that material.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	And sometimes it comes from percussion on the testicles, and this moisture is of many colors:
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	or it is colored declining to yellowishness, or it is without red, or black, or white and watery, and this can happen more.
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	and these are the signs to recognize this gathering, for if it is white mucus that we have said, it is a reasonable abscess, the swelling long like the shape of an egg, and does not open up the scrotum, because it has moisture all around.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if there is moisture in the natural fabric, then the abscess is reason with part of the egg, and because of this we think it's another yolk.
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	and if the moisture is between the skin of the scrotum and the white membrane, he senses it well;
donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	therefore when you want to know the color of the moisture, try it on all the introverted quadrilateral part from which the shape was before.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to these things then, that come after the introverted quarter, judge what is inside.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors;	And when we cut it out with iron, it is necessary that the patient be cleansed according to their power and the filling of their body;
puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	then sew him on his back, on something somewhat high, and put under him a lot of cloth bandage.
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions;	then sit on his left side, and instruct the attendant to sit on his right side, and extend the penis to one of its two sides near the skin of the scrotum.
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	Then take the spittle wet, and cut the skin of the buttocks between their length up to the finger's tip, and let your incision be entirely straight dividing the skin of the buttocks just so it becomes white, and scrape off gently according to one's power.
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont;	Then pierce the scrotum very carefully with an aqua needle to make a large hole, and extract all the water, and then put your needles in and stiffen the scrotum upwards.
et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement;	and do not touch the skin of the buttocks, but only the scrotum itself;
cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	cut it all out in one piece at once on both sides very carefully, lest if you do not cut well the water will return;
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac;	and if the testicle jumps out of its place during your work, then reset it in its place when you have completed the work on the scrotum;
puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then gather the two bookends of the scrotum at a suture, then heal it like other wounds, until they are healthy.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc;	And if you find the egg corrupted by another disease, it is necessary that you bind the vessels that are suspended, while binding back the bleeding.
puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	then tie the scrotum to all the suspended parts, and extract the egg, and heal it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices;	And if the testicle is torn into two parts together, know that they are two tendons.
si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	then tie the other part as you did to the first equaling, then clean out the bleeding, and put moistened linen in oil of roses into the wound.
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	and put another wet linen in wine and oil, and put over the two scrotums, and put on double-draped cloths, and tie above with all the thread which is according to this shape:
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil;	Then take two pieces of cloth, and sew them with yarn in the shape shown here, assembled by stitching in the crotch of the breeches; and one piece takes place on the fundament up to the back, and the other at the part of the elbow.
et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	and the other two pieces above the two armpits, and it should all be sewn together, encasing the restraint in the loop of the breeches.
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	and sometimes medicine is made with this sort of cauterizing in place of iron cutting, and it should be that you take one cauterizing needle fine, and scrape the skin from the scrotum, and heat it so as we have said, so that the white syrup that contains water is revealed.
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	if you take the cauterizing needle according to this shape, and pierce that syrup-like substance into the onces, and scrape it off with this fine hot cauterizer.
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout;	And the boil must be opened up in every way you can, until all is drained.
et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef;	and make sure that fire does not touch the egg.
et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve;	and know that this work is more safe;
et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	and be careful not to bleed, and do not neglect the works of cutting;
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	and if anything contrary happens to you, or an abscess bursts out or bleeding occurs, or another thing, cure what is happening against you, according to what has been said beforehand.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit;	And if the patient is fearful and does not want to undergo this operation because of its horror, give him a perforation, as I have told you, and it is that when you are well certain by the signs that we have said that this water is cold, then have the patient sit on a high seat;
pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors;	then pierce the abscess in the lower part right up to the entire length of the spine, and put the perforation deep into the body.
et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	and let the wound be wide so that all the water may flow forth;
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	then put cloth on the place and tie it, and let the remaining water flow out, then take care of him until the wound is healed;
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant;	and if the white cloth does not let the water flow out of the mouth of the wound, then you should insert a pin or an instrument with which one treats the water from dropsy, of which shape is shown above;
et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	and open up the pouch of the wound, and know that the water will return, and is assembled after six months or thereabouts, and when it is assembled as before, then the patient will pass their days;
de l’aposteme des coions	From the swelling of the testicles.
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	know that in the cutting of this thread there is fear of death in many dispositions, for which it seems to me that it is better to leave it alone;
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	and I will tell you the work and appearances of an abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions;	I say then that many abscesses come into the body, and indeed to the testicles;
et c’est par mout de cas.	and it is through many cases.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	It is to know by surplus of bitter and sharp humors which are spread to the testicles, or from bruising;
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors;	and the color of the abscess is according to the color of the body.
et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	and does not find any pain, and the abscess is heavy;
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	and by chance are certain abscesses heavy and painful and of a foul color, and sometimes come from the bursting of an artery or the swelling of a vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it is due to the bursting of an artery, it is known by the hot and swollen appearance of the abscess, when you press it with your fists;
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	And it does not seem fitting that you touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	He who is made from the inflowing of blood is known by his appearance to the touch of the hand, and can well make a cut above this resemblance, and above other tumors.
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	and cut the sac of the testicles, then the egg is on top, and the white cord of the scrotum, and deliver the suspensory from all parts of the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	If the egg is already hardened with these knots, then it is fitting that you cut the egg and the sac.
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	and if it is in the scrotum or in what is inside the pouches, then it is fitting that you deliver all that accumulation and cut around it.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the origin of the swelling is close to the back, then it is necessary that you cut all of it and pull out the sac, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your tasks are completed, apply the wound with damp wool in rose oil and vinegar, then cure it with other remedies until it is healed.
de l’aposteme des coions	From the swelling of the testicles.
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	This is an abscess enveloped in a wrapping similar to the scrotum, with the softening of the testicles, and the patient becomes seriously ill when it breaks.
et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	and the treatment of this disease is also quite fearful in like manner as before, and nonetheless we will tell you how to do it, according to what the ancient ones did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;	It is necessary that you have the patient sit on a high seat, then put the suspensory of the testicles down to your thighs, at all the vessels which are near to the penis, and bind the skin with bandages, and stretch them firmly.

puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	Then heal the wound as you do with others where a flesh wound becomes inflamed; so that neither pus nor bloody discharge nourishes one of the testicles.

de la routure dou syfac	...the treatment for hernia.
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The events of this hernia are by the incision which comes out through the scrotum, or by the extension above the belly in the part of the navel, because the intestines descend into that rupture to one of the testicles.
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes:	and this rupture is either through the scrotum, or from the extension of it, and these two manners come from different causes:
ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	of percussion, or a fall, or a blow, or a lifting of a heavy burden, and similar things;
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	and the signs when it is from a rupture of the sinew, are that there is a popping and a popping, over a long time, and does not come suddenly.
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	and the abscesses are equal all the way to the bottom, because the sinew presses against the intestine.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the sign is when it's a section from the navel that causes a sudden sharp pain at the beginning, and the swelling appears in various forms under the skin nearby, and this is because of the intestine coming out and the body being cut open from the front of the navel.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And at any time the intestines go into contact with the spleen, and are retained in this way, and cause great pain to suffer the patient, especially when it is pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these remedies of iron he should flee, because he wants to avoid them.

de hernie carnouse	It appears that the text is describing a medieval surgical procedure for treating a type of hernia.
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this place I have never seen anyone who dared to perform the treatment with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients said that it is made like the vine which grows around a stick, in such a manner as you bind gourds, after cutting them above lightly underneath;

et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then cure him as we have said, until he is healed.

et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	and do not let any of the intestines come out into the scrotum, and if they do come out, it is poor, and repair all hours;

Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The inflammation has subsided, and there is no appearance of the rupture, and the cauterization is useful in this place, and brings closer to healing.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	Concerning the softening of the skin of the scrotum
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	Many times is softened the skin of the testicles in certain men, because the stones that are inside are softened, and it is easy to see.
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	It is necessary, when one wants to cure it, that the patient be placed on their back, and a pad be applied to the natural skin which has been softened.
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	Then bring the two lips together at a suture, and if you see fit, sew up the excessiveness of the softened skin at three or four stitches.
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Then apply a dressing between the stitches, and the bandage as with other wounds, until it is healed, and have the thread cut.
dou chastrement	Concerning punishment.
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	Note that castration is forbidden in our law, and for this reason I would prefer not to speak of it in this book.
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	and it is only necessary by two methods:
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	one of which is that the physician in his wisdom will know how to answer when asked, and find the cure.
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	and the other, because we often have need of castration for certain animals to help us, such as goats and sheep and cats and other beasts.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	I instruct therefore that cauterization is done in two manners:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	or by attraction, or by incision.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	In the one that we do by attraction, let us cause the animal to sit in hot water until its limbs are softened and while.
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	then take them in your hand, as long as they are restored and you feel them no more.
Du chastrement de taille:	On the cauterization of size:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	it is necessary that you anoint the animal, and press the skin of its testicles in your left hand, then tie the suspensory ligament, and cut on each side to the scrotum when you have well scraped them;
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	and I leave no fat above it or the delicate skin that is over the vessels;
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	and this manner of cauterization is more wounding than the one that is done by attraction, because at the attraction there remains perhaps something from the testicles, by which the animal desires lust;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	then heal the wound until it is sound.
des hermofrodites	those who have a mixed sex (i.e., hermaphrodites)
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	Hermaproditism is in two ways among men:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	one is that between the two testicles it opens as well as the form of a woman's nature, or there are hairs and at times in front it discharges urine.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other manner is in women, and has on the thigh as well as a penis and two testicles.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	And the treatment of a man and a woman is that you cut the closed sinews altogether, and treat them as other wounds;
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	in the second way, men whose urine shoots through the skin of the testicles, have no treatment.
de la tentigene	of the unicorn
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	Tumescence is a closed cord above the natural part, as long as it is too ugly to see;
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	and some women have it just as large as a hand, and that's the treatment.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	You must cauterize the superfluity of the tumescence to your hand or with hot irons, and cut it lightly.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	And don't go too deep at first, lest bleeding occurs; then treat with another treatment until they are healed.
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	and there is another ulcer that forms at the mouth of the abscess, and it swells, and by chance bursts forth, and according to its resemblance it resembles a cow's udder, and for this reason they called it "cow sickness" in old times.
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	You must cover it, as we have said the incision, and heal it until it is sound.
de erratique	It seems you're reading from an old medical text. "De Erratique" doesn't appear to be a clear term, but I can try to translate the surrounding context.
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	 Erratic if the nature of the woman is not perceived, or the fistula is small;
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	and it is a natural thing by birth, or an accident that comes from illness.
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	or it is due to a hard abscess, or a subtle or thick fistula, and it forms deep in the abscess, or in the sides, or beneath, or wherever.
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	and obstructs conception, and childbirth, and by chance causes flowers to have;
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	And knowledge of this comes through the examination of the belly.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the swelling is nearby in appearance, it should be cut to your elbow or down to the rib.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	If it is a double fissure that is subtle and close to the two bones, then hurry and lance it thus:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	place your two index fingers together, and have the woman lie on her back, spread her legs;
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	then touch the two bones firmly, until the subtle fissure is closed, and the stoppages are over.
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	then take flax, and moisten it in oil, and place it on the bone, and support the woman at home each day, so that she cannot move.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the styptic is hard and thick, so you must steep the roots in vinegar similar to the leaves of myrtle.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	If the stoppages are of flesh, then suspend her at the armpit and lance it;
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	and have antihemorrhaging medicines, such as absinthe, blood of dragon, incense, together with abundance of egg.

et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	and thus it should be kept long, and give him a dry linen tent;
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then be cured with other treatments until he is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when in the thigh comes blood, it is necessary to strike it according to this manner, unless there are encysted abscesses.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For an encysted abscess in the thigh, one should not apply fire.
des emorroides	Piles (hemorrhoids)
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Morbid ulcers are openings of veins that, without scabbing as customary, and when morbid ulcers are old they become foul.
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	and we have already said in the division the similarities with them, and the signs, and I will say now those which receive cure.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and a thrombus, when they are deeply located in the rectum, and they do not appear to feel anything, except for treatment with iron.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those that are at the entrance of the rectum, which can be felt, are those that can be cured.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	It is therefore necessary that you put the woman in a cold house, then burn the athlum with tongs, and cut off its roots, then sprinkle on medicinal powders restraining blood, such as alum and dragon's blood and incense, and similar things.

et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	and if bleeding occurs from the cut, then have them sit in a decoction of sumac and pomegranate rind and gall and similar things; and then take barley flour and mix with honey and myrrh, and make it into a plaster on their back.

puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	then take linen and soak it in juice of plantain or in juice of hawthorn with old wine, and apply to the place.

des apostemes de la marris	Je comprends que vous voulez me poser une question plus spécifique.
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many kinds of abscess come to the navel, such as ulcers and pus-filled abscesses and herpetic blisters and fistulas and hemorrhoids and hot abscesses, and many other diseases that I have said in the division.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	It is therefore necessary that I say in this treatise the hot abscess which comes to the womb, which is not one of those that swell with pus.
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	and if you want to know the operation of iron, then look if the abscess is acute at its beginning of coming and full of heat and fever, and if it becomes red so that you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Then do not rush to incise it, but let it heal until the pain is relieved.
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	and then have the patient sit on a stool, and have two small stools so that he leans back, and lean on his back and bring his legs to the part behind the knee.
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	and let his thighs be spread wide, and place his arms under his knees, and tie them well with a good bandage.
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	Then the ball of the shoulder moves towards the right side, and with it comes the instrument with which we work on the mouth of the joint, from which this shape follows.
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	And it is necessary that when you go to apply this instrument, you make the first mark on the outside so as to know the depth of the joint, so that what goes into the instrument does not come further than it should and does not hurt the patient.
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	And if the instrument is larger, it is necessary to cover the depth of the joint with cloths, so that the instrument does not hurt him.
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	and he must put the cone of the instrument on top, and then shape the instrument.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	And when the abscess opens, and it is made to the hand soft, then it should be covered at the head, at the suppurative place.

de l’enfantement	Of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	it is necessary before the birth that she knows the figure of natural delivery, and the signs that are such that when you see the woman go down and desire to smell the air;
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	then the child hastens to force its way out;
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	then you should know that this childlike thing is according to the natural form, and it is the issue under its head, and the second part with it;
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	and when you see these signs, then it is necessary to press gently on its belly, so that the child comes out soon;
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	for when it rises up on its head, then the placenta goes with it, and the mother is freed of her excessences by good cleansing;
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	and this one that comes in another way does not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	For it sometimes comes up on its feet, and comes out through the body or the head, or the hands, or it comes up over the belly, or side, and is converted by chance over the neck, and by other bad forms;
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	so it is necessary for the midwife that she be wise and subtle in these things, and beware of error and deception, and I will show you all the forms how one must help her.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	If the child comes up over its head by natural delivery, and the woman gives birth grievously, and the virtues of it are weak, then make her sit on a saddle, or women hold her.
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	and anoint its nature with oil or fenugreek that is cooked, and then insert the ball between its shoulders a small spatula in this form:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	and cut the sinew, and chop at the joint so that the moisture which is inside comes out.
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	and paint the woman's belly so that the child descends, and if it does not descend, then you must purge the woman with fenugreek with oil of senna.
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	then make her hold and sneeze on condite, and keep her mouth and nose for an hour:
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	if it is now out the child.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	And if the two hands issue forth far, then you must gently reset them little by little.
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	and if they cannot enter, have the woman sit on top of it and lift up the feet high;
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	then dislodge the seat from the ground, and tie up the woman so she does not hinder the process.
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	and if the hands cannot enter and the fetus dies, then cut the hands with a knife that is put there beforehand, and take out the child, and reset it evenly.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	From the issue of the child on its feet.
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the fetus comes up to its feet, you should push it upwards;
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	and then turn it little by little until it is even.
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	then take the feet and stretch them little by little.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	As soon as it jumps up to the thighs, instruct her to grasp it, and make her hold tight from consideration.
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	If death occurs, may God will it.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if he is not further as we have said, then turn him little by little until he is according to the natural shape.

et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	and put on the natural condition of the woman inside and apply this ointment over it, then have her sit in warm water up to the armpits;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when she is moistened from below, then put a collar of myrrh around her and place it over her, and let her be for an hour;
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then have her sit on the birthing stool, then let her breathe and hold her mouth and nose, and touch her belly lightly, for the child is now leaping.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	from between her legs.
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the child comes in this form, then put a piece of cloth in its mouth pock and pock.
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	Then a bandage should be put on his neck, and the legs should hang down below, and he should lie on a bed.
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	and bend his hands inwards and outwards, and then he should press the hands on the abdomen, and remove the pillows underneath, until it is prepared downwards.
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	and if his child does not jump up, then take his feet and move them strongly, then move the belly upwards, then put your hands.
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	and bend the child inwards and outwards.
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	and command the woman to take hold of herself until the child comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	The issue of the child who comes out too wide is a hand during birth.
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	it is necessary to contrive to bring back the hand.
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	if one cannot bring it back, then make the woman sit up and go out;
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	if she cannot get up, then have her lie on the bed, and lift her legs strongly.
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	then administer the ointment which I have described.
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	and if it doesn't miscarry, then make her sit on the seat, and then study to bring back the hand;
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	and attend to the child according to its natural shape, and make it sneeze, and command her to take hold of herself until the birth comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	of the issue of the child on its neck, and it has spread out its hands, and its face is turned towards its mother's back.
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	it is necessary that the infant takes its hand, then turns it round and round, and attends to it lightly;
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	and when it is equal, then place on the natural ointment of aloes and oil, as we have said, then command her to move it round and round;
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	and when you have done that, then make her sit on the seat, and command her to take hold of herself.
et la fai esternuer.	and make it sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	by the same method for the entire second stage (of labor).
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When it comes out in this way the afterbirth, then cut the afterbirth at your finger, so that the moisture be emptied.
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and if the infant falls on its face and on its neck, then the head must be supported lest it be retained, and the infant perish.
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	then put the child inside, so that you have placed it as it should be, and instruct the woman to take hold of it once.
adonques si istra legierement.	then if it slips out lightly.
de l’issue des gemelz	of the birth of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	know that triplets are often born, and sometimes four;
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	and it is not a strange thing, and it often happens.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	Twins are a strange thing, and do not live if they be born;
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know that they, being multiplied, are divided by the uterus which divides them, which is attached to the belly;
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	and sometimes they come out naturally like any other children, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they grow quickly, then apply the treatment just as we have said, and the blister is subtle, and make what it does quickly and lightly;
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and do so likewise as it moves towards healing.
de plusors enfans	of several children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	Sometimes they are formed in the first or second or third or fourth or fifth or sixth or seventh degree, or more stages up to fifteen, and are all formed in the shape of an infant by the measurement of the wise surgeon, and it is necessary that the blister knows everything, for by chance similar things have happened;
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	do so according to what is required.
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you treat the woman after a stillbirth or miscarriage, as I said in the section on that, and no relief comes, and you are forced to operate manually;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	it is necessary that you know if the woman has a healthy uterus and does not have an accident or she fears death;
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	it is necessary that the woman be sitting on her back, and her head inclined downwards, and her legs lifted;
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	and the servant ties a cord of two parts around her waist, where she is tied to the bed so that she is not treated with the descent of the child;
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	then rub the mouth of the mother with moistened oils along with musk extract and fenugreek seed and flaxseed, then anoint her hands with these oils and these extracts;
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	then put them in the mother lightly, then look for a place where she can put the parts that are fitting to it, and take care if the child is prepared to descend on her head;
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	if the parts are inserted into her eyes or neck or mouth or palate or under the beard or in the navel or near the ribs, and if the descent is on the feet, then they insert or grasp it and cut off the edges;
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	It is necessary that the needle be in his right hand, and he puts the hook between his fingers of his left hand, and holds all his hand lightly, and drives the needle into any of those places which we have said, until it comes to the empty thing;
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	and this is the shape of the needle:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	then insert it against the other needle, or the third if you need one, so that the extraction be equal;
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then stretch it equally by moving one way and the other, for movement to come out, and so that the needles be bent for movement to hold, such as is its form:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if a part remains, take oil from some of his fingers and put it in that part, and pull the other part;
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	and if nothing remains, then place this needle or one higher in that place, and do thus until it comes out completely.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes in front of the other and he cannot move it back for grasping, you must wrap a cloth around it so that it comes out completely.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	then tie a strip in the joint of the foot or at the ankle, and thus you must do it with the other hand, and for both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the shoulder of the child is big and it sticks out at the exit, or it has an acute point assembled, then you must push a splint made of spine bone between your shoulders, and make the point and extract the tip.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	or you can mold it with the instrument called 'almidach', from which the shape comes with the instruments or chapter that is after this one.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and thus do likewise if the child has a large natural head.
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and then pull the bones apart with pincers, and if the shoulder jumps out and it sticks to the forcible, so that it is split, until the moisture which is in the joint comes out.
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if it cannot come out, then cut it with forceps that you can use.
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	and if there is swelling in the belly or under the ribs, you should make a small incision so that the moisture can drain.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the baby is on its feet, it's a gentle delivery, and the approach to the mouth of the womb is easy.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	and if it is a tumor in the belly or on the chest, you should extract it when it has been enveloped in cloth on the hand.
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and open the belly or the chest, until the moisture that is there drains out.
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	and if the other members are broken, and the head remains, then bind a band to his hand in front of the marrow, and pull it until it reaches the mouth of the marrow.
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	then insert oil or wine, and pull firmly.
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	and if the mouth of the marrow is constricted due to a hot abscess that has come there, then it is not necessary to intervene, but rather apply moist and greasy things.
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and the amnestra (plasters) of emollients, and soothings in warm water.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the fistula is on his ribcage and you can put him flat, then apply the plaster that we have said for a living infant.
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if they cannot be broken up, then cut them through with pieces and do not leave any of the secondary formation.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, then apply the plaster that we have said for cold abscesses which come in the groin.
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and if there comes out bleeding from the scab, then put it in a vinaigrette constricting and apply other treatments.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman in whose womb a dead baby had been placed, then she became pregnant with another on top of it, and the other died.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After long time the swollen abscess came on the cheek, and swelled so much that it burst open, and began to cause great inflammation.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was summoned to the cure, and I thought for long time, and could not heal the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I put on a poultice of great attraction, and from it came bones, and after some days another ones.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was greatly amazed, because the abdomen has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	So I thought it was the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I would cleanse the wound, and with gentle traction on the bones, until the woman was brought back to a better state.
