et puis la desloie, et rencomence une autre, tant que li nodations soit ostee;	and then loosen it, and apply another one, until the swelling is gone.
ou tu estrain sus une piece de plonc bien faite;	When you stretch over a piece of linen well-made;
car li proprietez dou plonc si est qu’il oste toutes les enfleures desus les membres;	for the properties of linen are such that it removes all swellings above the limbs;
et se li nodation est ja convertie en durteit ausi com piere, et il est besoing de l’oster, si la cope desus, et fent la superfluiteit apparent;	and if the inflammation has already turned to hardness like a stone and it is necessary to remove it, then cover it over and make the excess visible;
ou tu la reis a aucun raseur, tant qu’ele soit ostee, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee.	or you reset it with any rasor until it is removed, and care for it as long as it heals.
dou membre qui est foibles aprés la garison	from the limb that is weak after healing
Quant li brisure de l’os est restoree, et demoure aprés li membres foibles et subtilz, si avient por mout de causes:	When the break of the bone is restored, and remains after the limbs weak and subtle, it happens for many causes:
de coi l’une est por ceu qu’il fut liiez trop estroit, et ne fut mie liiez si com il covenoit;	because one is because it was tied too tightly, and not so as it ought to have been;
ou por ceu qu’il i ot trop de liiens, et ne pooit venir li norrissemens au membre;	or because there were too many bands, and the swelling could not come to the member;
ou por multitude d’arosement;	due to a surfeit of swelling.
ou por trop grans movements, ne mie en son houre;	or because of too great movement, not in its hour;
ou por ceu qu’il a poc de sanc en son cors, si est foibles.	or because he has much blood loss in his body, so he is weak.
Et li cure si est que tu faices mengier le malaide, et faire le cors tendre, tant que li sans soit multipliiez en lui;	And the treatment is that you make the patient eat and make their body soft, so that blood may be multiplied in them.
et li aministre bain, et li done joie et liesce;	and give them broth, and give them joy and comfort;
puis met poix sus le membre, si que li poix atraie a li grant norrissement, et l’arose sovent d’aigue tede, tant que li norrissement corre au membre;	then put poultice on the member, so that the poultice attracts to great swelling, and the moisture draws out often in thick liquid, until the swelling goes to the member.
et reviegne a sa figure natureil.	and recovers to its natural form.
dou membre tort aprés la santeit	from the twisted limb after healing
Quant li membres est tors aprés la restauration, et li os brisiez apert, et li forme dou membre est laide, toutevoie ne pert mie son ovraige natureil:	When the member is twisted after the restoration, and the bone is broken open, and the form of the member is ugly, nonetheless it does not lose its natural function.
si ne croire mie les folz qui dient c’on doit brisier lou membre tout de noveil, et maint fol mire ont ce fait en nostre terre;	Do not believe the fools who say that one must break off the member completely anew; and many foolish men have done this in our land.
et cist ovraiges est blamez, et en vient grans malz, et par aventure li mors;	and these works are blamed, and come to great evils, and perchance death.
toutevoie, se li nodations et li torture sont fres, si covient k’il soient arosez d’aigue chaude, ou herbes mollifians soient cuites, si com foilles de vismalve, et racines, et mellilote, et semblans choses;	nevertheless, if the swellings and tortures are fresh, it is necessary that they be washed with hot water, or herbs that soften things should be cooked, such as leaves of vervain, roots, and mallot, and similar things.
et li fai I emplaustre mollificatif, si com dyaquilon bien fait, et tu pren le muscillaige de vismalve, et la confit avec graisse de geline ou oile de sisament, et fai emplaustre sus;	and make a softening poultice, such as diacquilon well made, and take the juice of vervain, and boil it with goose fat or sesame oil, and make a poultice on it.
ou tu pren figues graisses, et les broie avec fien de colon, et semblans medicines que amenuisent le soudement.	or take fat figs, and grind them with coloquintida root, and similar medicaments that soften the swelling.
Et aucune fois est ostee li nodacion por froter continuelment et longement a mains moistes.	And at times is taken out the pustule by constant and long rubbing with wet hands.
Et soit amenistrez movement au membre chescune houre.	And let there be a movement to the member every hour.
Et se li tortuositez est enveillie et endurcie, ausi com piere, et besoins est de l’oster au fer, si la covient coper jusc’a l’os, a l’incisoire subtil legierement;	And if the twisting is hardened and turned to bone, like stone, and it needs to be removed with an iron, so you must cover it up just to the bone, lightly incising.
et mettre cusenson et estude en la cure.	and put a cautery and study in the treatment.
Ci encomence li livres des dislocations	Here begins the book of Dislocations.
Dislocations est issue d’aucune jointe de son leu, por coi il ne se puet muevre, et est li membres mal figurez, et sent li malaides grant dolor et grant lesion.	Dislocation is caused by a joint moving out of its place, so that it cannot move, and the limb is misaligned, and the patient feels great pain and great injury.
Quant dislocation vient a aucun, si le covient maintenant ramener sens targier.	When a dislocation occurs to anyone, if now it needs to be returned to its original position.
Car s’on tarde, si enfle li leus, et par aventure si le remet on a poines au leu;	For if you delay, the swelling will increase, and perhaps if you replace it the points will become stuck to the place;
por ceu ne covient mie c’on le mueve a l’oure k’il est enflez:	so therefore it is not necessary to move him until he has deflated.
maintes fois fait venir spame et autres dolors;	it has brought on spasms and other pains many times;
toutevoie, quant ce avenra, si fai sainier lou malaide, puis le laisse, tant que li apostemes chas soit apaisiez;	nevertheless, when this occurs, have the patient purged, then leave him alone until the abscess has been relieved.
puis arose le membre d’aigue chaude et d’oile, puis le ramoinne legierement, et cure chescun membre si com li cure venra en son leu.	then set the limb in warm water and oil, then reset it lightly, and treat each member as the treatment will come back to its place.
Et j’ai ordenez les chapistres des dislocations des lou chief jusc’a piez.	And I have ordered the chapters of dislocations from the head up to the foot.
des mandibules	of the jaw
Poc avient que les mandibules soient desaluees andous, et li dislocations d’ambedous est selonc II manieres:	The lower jawbone is often dislocated downward, and the dislocation of both jaws occurs in two ways:
ou elles sont un poc ostees de lor leus, et mollifies un poc;	or they are slightly out of their places, and somewhat softened.
ou elles sont desaluees entierement, et pendent vers lou pis, et cort li salive de la bouche qu’il ne la puet tenir, ne ne puet clore sa bouche, et envoloupe sa langue avec la parole.	or they are completely dislocated and hang towards the chin, and the saliva from the mouth flows out which it cannot hold, nor can it close its mouth, and it wraps around its tongue with its speech.
Quant li dislocations est petite, si revient par li em plusors disposicions.	When the dislocation is small, it heals in a few days.
Et s’elle est entiere et acomplie, si covient que tu la ramoinne hastanment, et ne targier mie;	And if it is complete and accomplished, then you must reset it promptly, and do not delay.
et en tel maniere que li ministres teigne le chief dou malaide, et boute li mires som pochet de l’une de ses mains en la racine de la dislocation de la mandibule dedens la bouche, se li dislocations est de II pars;	and in such a way that the minstrel holds the head of the patient, and inserts the mirror's sound pouch into one of his hands at the root of the jaw's dislocation inside the mouth, if the dislocation is on both sides.
et li autre doi des mains soient defuer, por mettre igal;	and with the other two hands be outside, to put it back in place.
et comande au malaide qu’il les amollisse, ses mandibules, et les mueve de toutes pars.	and instruct the patient to soften his jaws, and move them in all directions.
Et li mires la mete igal, tant qu’elle reveigne en son leu.	And the servants place the cloth equally on both sides, so that it returns to its place.
Et se li ramener est griés, meismement se ce sont les II mandibules ensamble, si les arose d’aigue chaude et d’oile, tant que les ramoinnes legierement;	And if it is stuck again, either in the two jaws together, so loosen them with hot water and oil, until they are loosened slightly.
ne ne targier mie dou ramener, si com nos avons dit.	do not at all touch the dislocation, as we have said.
Et quant elles sont ramenees igalment, et li bouche dou malaide clot bien sens mollifiier, si met sus drapelz moilliez en cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire, puis le lie legierement de molz liiens;	And when they are loosened evenly, and the patient's mouth has opened well and feels softened, put wet cloths on it in a poultice made of rose oil and wax, then bind it lightly with soft ties.
et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ses chiés soit estans entre II cussins, si qu’il ne lou mueve ne a destre ne a senestre, ne ne s’efforce mie de maixier, mais preigne legiere viande, tant que les dolors soient ostees, et soient noees les mandibules;	and the patient lies on his back, and his jaws are between two cushions, so that he neither moves them to the right nor to the left, nor does he try to chew, but takes light food, until the pains are removed, and the jaws are closed.
et puis menjuce ce qu’il vuet legierement, et ne se travaille mie d’ovrir la bouche au mengier et au boivre, tant que li mandibule soit bien noee et sanee.	And then moderate his diet slightly, and do not trouble yourself with opening the mouth to eat and drink, until the jawbone is well closed and healed.
Et se les .ij. mandibules ne pueent estre remises a point a une houre, et ne sont mie converties a lor leus, si en vient fievres et sode acostumees, et par aventure solution de ventre, et par aventure vomist cole pure.	And if the two mandibles cannot be put back in place within an hour and are not turned back to their positions, then fever and sharp stomachaches come, and perhaps intestinal purging, and perhaps vomiting of clean bile.
Et quant tu verras ceu, adonc saiches que c’est perdicions;	And when you see those, then know that it's a sign of death;
et maintes fois muert cil cui il avient, en VIIII jors.	and many times the person who has this dies within IX days.
de la forcelle	of the elbow
Li forcele ne puet desaluer dou costeit dedens la continuation de li et dou pis, et est desaluee aucune fois au defuer, et bien le sent on.	The elbow cannot be straightened from the inside towards the shoulder, and it is dislocated only once to the outside, and then one can feel it.
Et li restauration si est que li malaides gise sovin sor son dos, et estende ses bras;	And the treatment is that the patient lies often on his back and stretches out his arms;
et puis presse le leu forment a ta palme, et elle revenra;	and then press the place strongly against your palm, and it will return;
puis met sus l’emplaustre et lou bendeil, et l’estraint;	then put on the poultice and the bandage, and bind it;
et li chiez qui est devers lou coute ne puet desaluer;	and the bone that is near the rib cannot dislocate;
se poc non, et se il desalue aucune fois, si le ramoinne a son leu, si com nos avons dit;	it will not, and if it ever does dislocate, then reset it to its place, as we have said.
puis met sus l’emplaustre et le bendeil, et l’estraint, et coumande au malaide qu’il se repose tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then put on the plaster and bandage, and hold it, and instruct the patient to rest until they are healed.
et ensi meisme est ramenez li chiés de l’espale, quant il est desevrez de son leu.	and in the same way bring back the head of the scapula, when it is dislocated from its place.
de la dislocation de l’espaule	of the dislocation of the shoulder
Saiches que li espaule n’est desaluee fuer que selonc III manieres:	Know that the scapula is dislocated through three ways:
de coi l’une est qu’ele desalue a la partie de l’assele au desoz;	by which one it dislocates at the part of the armpit below;
et li seconde est a la partie dou pis;	and the second is in the area of the back.
et par aventure desalue a la partie desus, et ceu avient poc;	and by chance it dislocates at the top part, and this occurs rarely.
et ne desalue mie derrier por l’espaule, et ne desalue mie dedens por les ners;	and it does not dislocate behind for the shoulder, and it does not dislocate inside for the nerves.
et plusors fois desalue desoz vers l’assele, meismement a ces qui ont poc de char, car a ces saut ele fuer hastanment;	and often it dislocates downwards towards the armpit, precisely in those who have little fat, for in them it bursts forth quickly.
a ces qui ont assez char, saut ele a poines, et rentre a poines.	to those who have sufficient fat, there is the risk of abscess; it goes to points, and returns to points.
Et par aventure avient a aucuns homes percussion ou casseure, et enfle li espaule d’un aposteme chaut, et cuide qu’elle est desaluee par ceu.	And by chance it happens to some men that there is a blow or a crushing, and the shoulder swells with a hot tumor, and they think it is dislocated because of this.
Il covient donques que tu l’esprueves, tant que tu en soies certains;	you should then investigate it, until you are certain.
et adonques encomence la cure.	and then begin the treatment.
Et est conue li dislocations quant il est aval vers l’assele, et met difference entre l’espaule malade et la saine, et tu troveras entre lor diversiteit manifeste;	And it is known the dislocation when it falls towards the armpit, and makes a difference between the sick shoulder and the healthy one, and you will find a manifest diversity between them.
et troveras au chief de l’espaule une fosse, et desoz l’assele au tochier le chief de l’espaule, ausi com se ce soit uns oes;	and you will find at the top of the shoulder a pit, and under the armpit at the touch of the top of the shoulder, just as if it were an os.
et ne puet li malaides ramener sa main a son neis, ne movoir de nulz movemens;	and the patient cannot bring their hand to their neck, nor move with any movement.
et ausi, s’elle est desaluee en haut, si n’est mie occultee, car tu le trueves manifestement au tochier;	and similarly, if it is dislocated upwards, then it is not hidden, for you find it manifestly by feeling.
et ceste maniere de dislocation n’est mie fors a ramener, quant elle est novele, ou se li enfes est malaides.	and this manner of dislocation is not to be forced back, when it is new, unless the infant is ill.
Et li maniere est que li ministres lieve la main dou malaide en haut, puis met tes peuchas desoz l’assele, et lieve la jointure a force en haut au leu;	And the method is that the attendants lift the patient's hand up high, then place a pad under the elbow, and lift the joint with force up to its place;
et li ministres lieve la main, et l’estende en haut, pues le mette desoz;	and the attendants lift the hand, and stretch it up high, then put a cloth under it.
si venra hastanment.	if it comes quickly.
Et s’elle ne vient si com nos avons dit em mains jors aprés, si covient ke li malaides soit baigniez en aigue chaude;	And if it does not come as we have said within a few days, then the patient must be bathed in hot water;
et li amenistre arosement mollifiant et assouajant, si com decoction de altee et de fenugrec et de mellilote en aigue, et soit amenistree;	and the administrator must administer it soothingly and calming, such as a decoction of marjoram and dill and melilot in water, and be brought.
puis soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos, et mette on desoz l’assele un sto de lainne igal, ne trop mol ne trop dur, puis mette li mires son talon sus le sto, et lieve le chief de l’espaule vertuousement, et traie la main dou malaide;	then the patient is to be supported on their back, and a piece of linen cloth is placed under the elbow, not too soft nor too hard, then the physician puts his heel over the cloth, and raises the head of the shoulder forcefully, and pulls the hand of the patient.
et uns autres ministres teigne lou chief dou malaide, si qu’il ne se mueve aval;	and another attendant ties a cloth over the patient's head, so that it does not move downward.
celle espaule revient tout maintenant, et se tu vues si le ramoinne selonc ceste maniere:	the shoulder returns to its place immediately, and if you see it, then you must reset it in this manner:
et est que tu faices estre present I home qui soit plus grans que li malaides;	and that you have someone come who is larger than the patient;
et soit drois devers lou costeit, et boute s’espaule desoz l’assele dou malaide, et lieve l’assele en haut, si que li malaides pende en l’ar;	and he should stand straight over the patient and place his shoulder under the beam of the patient, and lift up the beam so that the patient hangs in the air;
et uns autres ministres traie la main dou malaide aval devers lou ventre.	and another attendant takes hold of the patient's hand down towards the belly.
Et se li malaides est trop legiers, si pent avec lui aucune chose pesant, et li dislocation revient maintenant.	And if the patient is too light, he can carry something heavy with him, and the dislocation will return now.
Et le ramoinne on ausi en autre maniere:	And you reset it in another manner as well:
et est c’on fiche I lonc tison en terre, dont li chiés soit ausi reons com I pistal, et ne soit ne trop gros ne trop graile;	and is that one puts a long iron rod into the ground, so that the tip is as red-hot as a burning stick, and not too large nor too thick;
puis soit mis desoz lou malaide, mais k’il ait drapelz souef sus, et li malaides soit estans dou lonc dou fust;	then it is put under the patient, but so that it is wrapped softly on top, and the patient stands away from the length of the rod.
puis soit estendue sa main aval d’autre part forment, et li jointure revenra en son leu hastanment;	Then let his hand be extended downward from the other side, forming a joint that will return to its place quickly.
et s’elle ne vuet revenir por toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si fai ceste cure:	and if it does not want to return for all the things that we have said, then do this treatment:
pren I tison de II bras de grant et IIII dois de large, qui ait le chief reont por mues entrer em parfont desoz l’assele, selonc ceste forme:	take a stick from two arms of great and four fingers in width, which has the head round so that it can be plunged into the depth below the shoulder, according to this shape:

Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les II piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les II talons, et sus les II genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue II dois plus que li autres;	And if you cannot compress it in this manner as we have said, then it is necessary that you tie the two legs of the patient together with a strong soft lien above the two heels, and on the two knees, and let the sick leg be extended two thumbs more than the others;
puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre II bras de lonc;	then it should be hung up from the head of a beam, and should be above the ground at a length of two arms.
puis comande a I ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.	then command the minister to take hold of the head of the thigh, and let another minister hang with the patient, who should take hold strongly of the thigh, because the joint is now returning quickly.
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	And when the dislocation is at its worst, have the patient lie down as we said in the case of sciatica, and straighten the leg properly above the ailing knee, as well above the hip.
puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	then place two burning torches, one at the head and the other at the feet, then insert a burning stick between the patient's thighs in the middle.
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	and have wet rags wrapped around so that the patient does not get burned, then each assistant stretch towards him and the surgeon place his hand even with the patient's hand on the dislocation.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	If it returns, that's good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	If not, put them on the table and press them thus as we have said in the Galenism, and place the patient on the right side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;	And when the dislocation is in front, it is necessary to extend the ailing leg hastily, and according to what I have said.
et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	and the surgeon puts his hand over the knee of the patient, then presses with the other hand and stretches it downwards towards the ankle.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;	And if the dislocation is high, it should not extend the patient below, nor raise above the earth, but rather be as if the hip were dislocated to the side, as we have said about lying on two hips;
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	and it should be above his face, and the bandage should be extended as we have said before, and he must be pressed on the joint at the table;
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;	and it will be level when the patient stretches out his legs, and they will be even;
adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	then bring the thighs together, and apply a poultice, and bind with a bandage, so that the hip does not move;
et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;	and if he rests for three days or four, then unfasten it, and apply a poultice on top;
et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;	and if you see that they are even, then bind him, as before, and let him rest for three days;
puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	Then loosen it, and make it go gently, until the limbs are comfortable.
de la dislocation dou genoil	of the dislocation of the knee
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	The jaw is dislocated in three manners:
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	that is to say, inward and outward, and behind.
et ne desalue point devant.	and it does not dislocate forward.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	And the sign is that you instruct the patient to bend their leg at the knee, and if it does not bend at the knee, know that it is dislocated.
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	and the restoration of all is that you make the patient sit upright, and stretch their leg if they can, and place your back on their face, and place their foot on yours.
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment;	then take their knee to your palms, and pull it between your fingers, then bend the two sides of the knee together.
et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	and another assistant stretches his foot, until the jaw returns to its place, and the sign is that it bends well at the knee slightly.
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;	and place the poultice on it, and heat the leg to the knee, and bind them together tightly for three or four days, then loosen.
et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	and do not trouble the patient to go anywhere, until the members are comforted.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the member is not in place, administer strong stretching, as we have said in the treatment of the hip, until it is healed.
de la dislocation dou talon	of the dislocation of the heel
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heel is sometimes sprained and sometimes completely dislocated, both inward and outward.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	And the signs are that the ankle is swollen, and tense before the part where it was dislocated:
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	the return to its place is easy, and one should extend the limb lightly with their hands when it is only being reduced.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	And when it is dislocated completely, it is necessary that you make the patient sit straight, and bind him tightly with bandages from the leg, above the ankle.
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	then draw the foot to you with your right hand, and then twice with your left hand, then stretch it up high, and put the foot back up high.
et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	and do this twice, as we have said, with pushing and with drawing out the foot;
s’elle revient, c’est bien;	if it returns, it's well;
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	if not, then repeat the work, because it will return;
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	and if it cannot return like that, then have the patient lie on his back on the ground, and put a staff firmly in the earth between his thighs, and tie up cloths around him, so that he will not hurt himself;
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	then have the minister take hold of the thigh, and another minister extend the foot to his hands or to the strap, so that he ties on the ankle of the foot;
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	then have each minister stretch equally, and the staffs should be there between the thighs of the patient to hold back the patient when you are stretching it;
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	then place the fingers of the suture equally on the dislocation in his hands, and another minister takes hold of the healthy leg below, and the dislocation will return quickly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	And when it is applied to the point, place a poultice and compress on top, and hold firmly, tie the foot to the leg, and guard the nerves that are above the heel behind, so that the bandage is not too tight;
puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	then let it be for 2 days or 3, and if the compress loosens, re-tie;
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	then release it on the fourth day or the fifth, and have the patient abstain from going for 4 days;
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	and if he goes before that time period is ended, it is not certain that it will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if an abscess forms on the heel, it is advisable that you treat it, as we have said elsewhere, until it is sound.
des dois	of the toes
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the toes are dislocated, they should be gently stretched without force, and it is a slight thing.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	And if the dislocation is in any part of the back of the foot, it is necessary that you have the patient sit on a flat place or on a table completely straight, and place your foot over what appears of those joints, then press firmly with your foot until it returns.
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	And when it is level and there is no opening, place under the sole of the foot a board with two pegs, then tie it firmly, and let it stay three days, then release.
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and have him rest until he is healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	of wounds and dislocations together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When a wound comes with the dislocation, and one wants to restore it, many times the patient dies:
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	be not presumptuous in the treatment, if you are not wise in the art and have not practiced it for a long time, and if you are not compassionate and merciful and slow, nor too hasty;
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	and at the beginning treat the warm abscess with soothing things, and leave the patient in God's hand, if you do not see hope of healing.
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	and when you see hope, then now reset the member to its place, so that the hot abscess will come;
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	and when the limb is back in place, administer warm poultices to the abscess and treat the wound as it should be done with drying ointments.
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	and if the dislocation has a break and small bones are fractured, separate the bones, and do what we have said in simple diseases;
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	and beware of entering into a way of fear, as I have said, for it is worth nothing to you according to your creator, and for the knowledge to protect yourself and your body.
